# Purgatorio - Canto 7

### 1 Poscia che l’accoglienze oneste e liete

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: After the courteous and joyful greetings
- **gemini1-ja**: 丁重で嬉しい歓迎が

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: Afterwards that the honest and joyful welcomes
- **gemma3-ja**: それから、丁寧で喜ばしい挨拶が
<table>
<tr><th>Word</th><td>Poscia</td><td>che</td><td>l'</td><td>accoglienze</td><td>oneste</td><td>e</td><td>liete</td></tr>

**gptoss-it**
- **gptoss-en**: After that the honest and joyful welcomes  
- **gptoss-ja**: その後、正直で喜ばしい歓迎が

### 2 furo iterate tre e quattro volte,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: had been repeated three and four times,
- **gemini1-ja**: 3度か4度繰り返された後、

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: were repeated three and four times,
- **gemma3-ja**: 三度、四度繰り返された後、

### 3 Sordel si trasse, e disse: «Voi, chi siete?».

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: Sordello stepped forward and said: "Who are you?".
- **gemini1-ja**: ソルデルが前に出てきて言った。「あなた方はどなたですか？」

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: Sordel withdrew, and said: “You, who are you?”
- **gemma3-ja**: ソルデルは身を引き、言った。「あなた方は誰ですか？」

<tr><th>Latin</th><td>Sordellus</td><td>se</td><td>traxit</td><td>et</td><td>dixit</td><td>vos</td><td>quis</td><td>estis</td></tr>

**gptoss-it**
- **gptoss-en**: Sordel drew himself, and said: “You, who are you?”.
- **gptoss-ja**: ソルデルは身を引き、言った：「あなた方、誰ですか？」

### 4 «Anzi che a questo monte fosser volte

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: Before the souls worthy of ascending to God
- **gemini1-ja**: この山に登って
<table>
<tr><th>Word</th><td>Anzi</td><td>che</td><td>a</td><td>questo</td><td>monte</td><td>fosser</td><td>volte</td></tr>

<tr><th>Tense</th><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>past imperfect</td><td>past participle</td></tr>
<tr><th>Mood</th><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>subjunctive</td><td></td></tr>
<tr><th>English</th><td>rather</td><td>than</td><td>to</td><td>this</td><td>mountain</td><td>were</td><td>turned</td></tr>
<tr><th>Latin</th><td>antea</td><td>quam</td><td>ad</td><td>iste</td><td>mons</td><td>esse</td><td>voltare</td></tr>
<tr><th>Interlingua</th><td>ante</td><td>que</td><td>a</td><td>iste</td><td>monte</td><td>esser</td><td>voltar</td></tr>
<tr><th>French</th><td>plutôt</td><td>que</td><td>à</td><td>ce</td><td>mont</td><td>être</td><td>tourner</td></tr>
<tr><th>Spanish</th><td>antes</td><td>que</td><td>a</td><td>este</td><td>monte</td><td>fueron</td><td>voltear</td></tr>
<tr><th>Portuguese</th><td>antes</td><td>que</td><td>a</td><td>este</td><td>monte</td><td>foram</td><td>virar</td></tr>
<tr><th>Romanian</th><td>mai degrabă</td><td>decât</td><td>la</td><td>acesta</td><td>munte</td><td>erau</td><td>întoarce</td></tr>
<tr><th>Esperanto</th><td>pli frue</td><td>ol</td><td>al</td><td>ĉi tiu</td><td>monto</td><td>estis</td><td>turni</td></tr>

<tr><th>Etymology</th><td>antea</td><td>quid</td><td>ad</td><td>eccu(m) + iste</td><td>montem</td><td>esse</td><td>voltare</td></tr>
</table>

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: Before that to this mountain were turned
- **gemma3-ja**: この山に昇るに値する魂よりもむしろ
<table>

### 19 qual merito o qual grazia mi ti mostra?

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: what merit or what grace shows you to me?
- **gemini1-ja**: どんな功績や恩恵があって、私にあなたを見せてくれるのですか？

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: what merit or what grace do you show to me?
- **gemma3-ja**: どのような功績、またはどのような恵みが私にあなたを見せるのか？

### 21 dimmi se vien d’inferno, e di qual chiostra».

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: tell me if you come from hell, and from which circle."
- **gemini1-ja**: 地獄から来たのか、どの圏層から来たのか教えてください。」

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: tell me if you come from hell, and from what cloister.”
- **gemma3-ja**: 私に言ってください、あなたは地獄から来たのか、そしてどの修道院から来たのか？」

### 24 virtù del ciel mi mosse, e con lei vegno.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: the power of heaven moved me, and with it I come.
- **gemini1-ja**: 天の力が私を動かしたのです。そして、その力と一緒にやって来ました。

### 25 Non per far, ma per non fare ho perduto

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: Not for doing, but for not doing, have I lost
- **gemini1-ja**: 行動するためではなく、行動しないために私は失った

### 42 per quanto ir posso, a guida mi t’accosto.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: as far as I can go, I will accompany you as your guide.
- **gemini1-ja**: 行ける限り、私はあなたを導く。」

### 43 Ma vedi già come dichina il giorno,

### 44 e andar sù di notte non si puote;

- **gemini1-ja**: 夜に上るのは不可能だ。

### 46 Anime sono a destra qua remote;

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: There are souls to the right here, withdrawn;
- **gemini1-ja**: 右側には人里離れた魂たちがいる。

### 96 sì che tardi per altri si ricrea.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: so that it is too late for her to be revived by others.
- **gemini1-ja**: それは他の者によって遅すぎるほど遅れて行われた。

### 98 resse la terra dove l’acqua nasce

### 99 che Molta in Albia, e Albia in mar ne porta:

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: that the Moldau carries into the Elbe, and the Elbe into the sea:
- **gemini1-ja**: モルタ川がアルビア川に、アルビア川が海に運ぶ水

### 100 Ottacchero ebbe nome, e ne le fasce

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: his name was Ottokar, and in his swaddling clothes
- **gemini1-ja**: オッターケーロという名前で、おむつの頃

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: He had the name Ottacher, and in his swaddling clothes
- **gemma3-ja**: オッターケロという名前を持ち、彼の帯の中で

### 106 guardate là come si batte il petto!
